with configuration in protobuf definitions. The `HttpConnectionManager` message is defined in both v3 (`envoy/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/v3/http_connection_manager.proto`) and v2 (`envoy/config/filter/network/http_connection_manager/v2/http_connection_manager.proto`) versions. These proto messages contain the `filter_chains` field that defines which HTTP filters should be applied to incoming requests.\\n\\nThe `FilterChainFactory` interface (in `envoy/http/filter_factory.h`) is the abstract base for creating HTTP filter chains. It defines two main methods:\\n- `createFilterChain()`: Called when a new HTTP stream is created on the connection\\n- `createUpgradeFilterChain()`: Called when a new upgrade stream is created\\n\\nThe concrete implementation of `FilterChainFactory` is provided by `HttpConnectionManagerConfig` (in `source/extensions/filters/network/http_connection_manager/config.h`). This class inherits from both `Http::FilterChainFactory` and `Http::ConnectionManagerConfig`, and it processes the protobuf configuration to build the filter chain.\\n\\n## Configuration Processing\\n\\nThe `FilterChainHelper` template class (in `source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h`) is responsible for processing filter configurations at initialization time. It takes the `HttpFilter` messages from the proto configuration and creates `FilterFactoryCb` callbacks for each filter. The `FilterChainUtility` class (also in `filter_chain_helper.h`) provides the static method `createFilterChainForFactories()` which orchestrates the creation of the filter chain from a list of factory callbacks.\\n\\nThe `FilterChainManager` interface (in `envoy/http/filter_factory.h`) acts as the \\\"sink\\\" where filter factories can post their filters. The main method is `applyFilterFactoryCb()` which accepts a `FilterContext` and a `FilterFactoryCb` callback.\\n\\nThe `FilterFactoryCb` is a function type that takes `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks&` as a parameter. Individual filter factories return these callbacks during initialization, which are then called at stream creation time.\\n\\n## Execution Phase\\n\\nAt runtime, when a new HTTP stream is created, the `ConnectionManagerImpl` (in `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h`) - which implements the `Network::ReadFilter` interface - triggers filter chain creation by calling `createFilterChain()` on the configured `FilterChainFactory` (HttpConnectionManagerConfig). \\n\\nThe `FilterManager` class (in `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`) is responsible for executing the filter chain at runtime. It maintains the state of stream filters and manages their lifecycle. The `FilterManager::createFilterChain()` method calls the factory callbacks to instantiate the actual filter objects.\\n\\nThe `DownstreamFilterManager` (in `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`) extends `FilterManager` with explicit handling for sending local replies to the client.\\n\\nThe `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks` interface (in `envoy/http/filter.h`) provides the callbacks that filter factories use to add their filters to the chain:\\n- `addStreamDecoderFilter()`: Adds filters that process incoming request data\\n- `addStreamEncoderFilter()`: Adds filters that process outgoing response data\\n- `addStreamFilter()`: Adds bidirectional filters\\n- `addAccessLogHandler()`: Adds access log handlers\\n- `dispatcher()`: Provides access to the thread-local dispatcher\\n\\n## Complete Flow\\n\\n1. **Configuration Loading**: Protobuf config specifies filter_chains in HttpConnectionManager message\\n2. **Initialization**: HttpConnectionManagerConfig and FilterChainHelper process the config and create FilterFactoryCb callbacks\\n3. **Stream Creation**: When a new HTTP stream arrives, ConnectionManagerImpl calls HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain()\\n4. **Filter Instantiation**: FilterManager calls the FilterFactoryCb callbacks which invoke FilterChainFactoryCallbacks::addStreamDecoderFilter/Encoder/Filter()\\n5. **Runtime Execution**: FilterManager orchestrates the execution of the filter chain, passing data through each filter in sequence\\n\\nThe key architectural pattern is the use of factory callbacks (`FilterFactoryCb`) that are created at configuration time but called at stream creation time. This allows for efficient filter instantiation with proper lifecycle management while maintaining separation between configuration and stream-specific behavior.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":6215,"cache_read_input_tokens":86380,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":6215},"output_tokens":6,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e34911c5-bc5d-4e85-958e-ce58ac1ca0ca","uuid":"2000bd1e-88fb-4a6f-955f-0e885676e45c"}

Individual filter factories return these callbacks during initialization, which are then called at stream creation time.\\n\\n## Execution Phase\\n\\nAt runtime, when a new HTTP stream is created, the `ConnectionManagerImpl` (in `source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h`) - which implements the `Network::ReadFilter` interface - triggers filter chain creation by calling `createFilterChain()` on the configured `FilterChainFactory` (HttpConnectionManagerConfig). \\n\\nThe `FilterManager` class (in `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`) is responsible for executing the filter chain at runtime. It maintains the state of stream filters and manages their lifecycle. The `FilterManager::createFilterChain()` method calls the factory callbacks to instantiate the actual filter objects.\\n\\nThe `DownstreamFilterManager` (in `source/common/http/filter_manager.h`) extends `FilterManager` with explicit handling for sending local replies to the client.\\n\\nThe `FilterChainFactoryCallbacks` interface (in `envoy/http/filter.h`) provides the callbacks that filter factories use to add their filters to the chain:\\n- `addStreamDecoderFilter()`: Adds filters that process incoming request data\\n- `addStreamEncoderFilter()`: Adds filters that process outgoing response data\\n- `addStreamFilter()`: Adds bidirectional filters\\n- `addAccessLogHandler()`: Adds access log handlers\\n- `dispatcher()`: Provides access to the thread-local dispatcher\\n\\n## Complete Flow\\n\\n1. **Configuration Loading**: Protobuf config specifies filter_chains in HttpConnectionManager message\\n2. **Initialization**: HttpConnectionManagerConfig and FilterChainHelper process the config and create FilterFactoryCb callbacks\\n3. **Stream Creation**: When a new HTTP stream arrives, ConnectionManagerImpl calls HttpConnectionManagerConfig::createFilterChain()\\n4. **Filter Instantiation**: FilterManager calls the FilterFactoryCb callbacks which invoke FilterChainFactoryCallbacks::addStreamDecoderFilter/Encoder/Filter()\\n5. **Runtime Execution**: FilterManager orchestrates the execution of the filter chain, passing data through each filter in sequence\\n\\nThe key architectural pattern is the use of factory callbacks (`FilterFactoryCb`) that are created at configuration time but called at stream creation time. This allows for efficient filter instantiation with proper lifecycle management while maintaining separation between configuration and stream-specific behavior.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
